-- Total: 15549 blocks
function f()
	while not turtle.forward() do
		if turtle.detect() then
			turtle.dig()
		end
	end
end
function u()
	while not turtle.up() do
		if turtle.detectUp() then
			turtle.digUp()
		end
	end
end
function d()
	while not turtle.down() do
	end
end
function l()
	turtle.turnLeft()
end
function r()
	turtle.turnRight()
end
function p()
	turtle.placeDown()
end
function s(slot)
	turtle.select(slot)
end
function sk()
	turtle.suck()
end
function dr()
	turtle.drop()
end
function rl()
	turtle.refuel()
end
function fl()
	return turtle.getFuelLevel()
end
